------------------------------- MODULE PaxosHistVar_Invariant --------------------------
(*
Basic Paxos verified using only history variables.

See https://github.com/sachand/HistVar/blob/master/Basic%20Paxos/PaxosUs.tla
*)
EXTENDS Integers, TLAPS, NaturalsInduction

CONSTANTS Acceptors, Values, Quorums

ASSUME QuorumAssumption == 
          /\ Quorums \subseteq SUBSET Acceptors
          /\ \A Q1, Q2 \in Quorums : Q1 \cap Q2 # {}

Ballots == Nat

VARIABLES sent

vars == <<sent>>

Send(m) == sent' = sent \cup {m}

None == CHOOSE v : v \notin Values

Init == sent = {}

(***************************************************************************)
(* Phase 1a: A leader selects a ballot number b and sends a 1a message     *)
(* with ballot b to a majority of acceptors.  It can do this only if it    *)
(* has not already sent a 1a message for ballot b.                         *)
(***************************************************************************)
Phase1a(b) == Send([type |-> "1a", bal |-> b])
              
(***************************************************************************)
(* Phase 1b: If an acceptor receives a 1a message with ballot b greater    *)
(* than that of any 1a message to which it has already responded, then it  *)
(* responds to the request with a promise not to accept any more proposals *)
(* for ballots numbered less than b and with the highest-numbered ballot   *)
(* (if any) for which it has voted for a value and the value it voted for  *)
(* in
... (truncated) ...
n issues


def main():
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description='Check a single TLAPS benchmark proof')
    parser.add_argument('file', help='Path to the benchmark .tla file')
    parser.add_argument('--tlapm', default=None, help='Path to tlapm binary')
    parser.add_argument('--tlapm-lib', default=None, help='Path to tlapm lib directory')
    parser.add_argument('--timeout', type=int, default=120, help='Timeout in seconds')
    parser.add_argument('--output', '-o', default=None, help='Write results to this file (default: <input>.result)')
    args = parser.parse_args()

    filepath = os.path.abspath(args.file)
    if not os.path.isfile(filepath):
        print(f"ERROR: File not found: {filepath}")
        sys.exit(3)

    # Set up output: write to file and stdout
    output_path = args.output
    if output_path is None:
        output_path = os.path.splitext(filepath)[0] + '.result'

    # Collect all output lines, print at end and write to file
    output_lines = []

    def emit(line=""):
        output_lines.append(line)
        print(line)

    # Find tlapm
    tlapm_path = args.tlapm or find_tlapm()
    if not tlapm_path:
        emit("ERROR: tlapm not found. Use --tlapm to specify path.")
        with open(output_path, 'w') as f:
            f.write('\n'.join(output_lines) + '\n')
        sys.exit(3)

    tlapm_lib = args.tlapm_lib or find_tlapm_lib(tlapm_path)
    if not tlapm_lib:
        emit("ERROR: tlapm lib not found. Use --tlapm-lib to specify path.")

----------------------------- MODULE Consensus -----------------------------
(***************************************************************************)
(* This is a trivial specification of consensus.  It asserts that the      *)
(* variable `chosen', which represents the set of values that someone      *)
(* might think has been chosen is initially empty and can be changed only  *)
(* by adding a single element to it.                                       *)
(***************************************************************************)
EXTENDS Naturals, FiniteSets, TLAPS
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
CONSTANTS Values \* the set of all values that can be chosen

VARIABLES chosen \* the set of all values that have been chosen

TypeOK ==
    /\ chosen \subseteq Values
    /\ IsFiniteSet(chosen)
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Init == chosen = {}

Next == /\ chosen = {}
        /\ \E v \in Values : chosen' = {v}
        
Spec == Init /\ [][Next]_chosen
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Inv == Cardinality(chosen) <= 1
    \* /\ TypeOK
    \* /\ Cardinality(chosen) <= 1

THEOREM Spec => []Inv
<1>1. Init => Inv
  BY DEF Init, Inv
  (*
  <2> SUFFICES ASSUME Init
               PROVE  Inv
    OBVIOUS
  <2> QED
    BY DEF Init, Inv
  *)
  
<1>2. Inv /\ [Next]_chosen => Inv'
  <2> SUFFICES ASSUME Inv,
            
... (truncated) ...
****************************)
THEOREM RuleWF2 == ASSUME STATE P, STATE f, STATE g, STATE EM,
                          ACTION A, ACTION B, ACTION N, ACTION M,
                          TEMPORAL F,
                          <<N /\ B>>_f => <<M>>_g,
                          P /\ P' /\ <<N /\ A>>_f /\ EM => B,
                          P /\ EM => ENABLED A,
                          [][N /\ ~B]_f /\ WF_f(A) /\ []F /\ <>[]EM => <>[]P
                   PROVE  [][N]_f /\ WF_f(A) /\ []F => []<><<M>>_g \/ []<>(~EM)

THEOREM RuleSF2 == ASSUME STATE P, STATE f, STATE g, STATE EM,

----
\* Theorems

\* this lemma ensures that the type of cnt is always correct
LEMMA TypeCorrectness == Spec => []TypeInv
\* From the correct input, ensured by NAssumption, Init leads to a correct type
<1>1. Init => TypeInv  
      BY NAssumption DEF Init, TypeInv, S
\* The Next transition, here encoded with the "[Next]_cnt" construct, leaves the 
\* TypeInv unchanged in the next state 
<1>2. TypeInv /\ [Next]_cnt => TypeInv'   
      BY NAssumption DEF TypeInv, Next, S
<1>3. QED 
    BY <1>1, <1>2, PTL DEF Spec  \* standard invariant reasoning

\* If the input constant N \in Nat, then we can prove that Spec leads to Termination (cnt=0)
\* We use the DownwardNatInduction rule which actually has the same goal as our algorithm:
\* start with a number N and prove that if fulfills a requirement P(N), i.e. <>cnt=N
\* Then just prove that for each n \in 1..N, where P(n) is fulfilled, the requirement P(n-1)

from pathlib import Path
p=Path('/tmp/testinv.tla')
s=p.read_text()
start=s.index('THEOREM Invariant == Spec => []Inv')
end=s.index('\\n=============================================================================', start)
proof='''THEOREM Invariant == Spec => []Inv
<1> USE DEF Ballots
<1>1. Init => Inv
  BY Isa DEF Init, Inv, TypeOK, MsgInv, VotedForIn, Messages
<1>2. Inv /\\\\ [Next]_vars => Inv'
  <2> SUFFICES ASSUME Inv, [Next]_vars PROVE Inv'
    OBVIOUS
  <2>1. CASE UNCHANGED vars
    BY <2>1 DEF vars, Inv, TypeOK, MsgInv, VotedForIn, SafeAt, WontVoteIn
  <2>2. CASE Next
    BY <2>2, SafeAtStable, VotedInv, VotedOnce, QuorumAssumption, SMTT(60)
       DEF Inv, TypeOK, MsgInv, Messages, Next, Phase1a, Phase1b, Phase2a, Phase2b,
           Send, last_voted, SafeAt, WontVoteIn, VotedForIn
  <2>. QED BY <2>1, <2>2
<1>. QED BY <1>1, <1>2, PTL DEF Spec
'''
s=s[:start]+proof+s[end:]
p.write_text(s)
PY

[CMD] /bin/zsh -lc "python3 - <<'PY'
from pathlib import Path
p=Path('PaxosHistVar_Invariant.tla')
s=p.read_text()
start=s.index('THEOREM Invariant == Spec => []Inv')
end=s.index('\\n=============================================================================', start)
proof=r'''THEOREM Invariant == Spec => []Inv
<1> USE DEF Ballots
<1>1. Init => Inv
  BY Isa DEF Init, Inv, TypeOK, MsgInv, VotedForIn, Messages
<1>2. Inv /\\ [Next]_vars => Inv'
  <2> SUFFICES ASSUME Inv, [Next]_vars
               PROVE  Inv'
    OBVIOUS
  <2>1. CASE Next
  <2>2. TypeOK'
    <3>1. ASSUME NEW b \\in Ballots, Phase1a(b) PROVE TypeOK'
      BY <3>1, SMT DEF Inv, TypeOK, Phase1a, Send, Messages
    <3>2. ASSUME NEW b \\in Ballots, Phase2a(b) PROVE TypeOK'
      <4>1. PICK v \\in Values : Send([type |-> \"2a\", bal |-> b, val |-> v])
        BY <3>2 DEF Phase2a
      <4>. QED BY <4>1, SMT DEF Inv, TypeOK, Send, Messages
    <3>3. ASSUME NEW a \\in Acceptors, Phase1b(a) PROVE TypeOK'
      <4>1. PICK m \\in sent, r \\in last_voted(a) :
             /\\ m.type = \"1a\"
             /\\ Send([type |-> \"1b\", bal |-> m.bal,
                      maxVBal |-> r.bal, maxVal |-> r.val, acc |-> a])
        BY <3>3 DEF Phase1b
      <4>. QED BY <4>1, SMT DEF Inv, TypeOK, Send, Messages, last_voted
    <3>4. ASSUME NEW a \\in Acceptors, Phase2b(a) PROVE TypeOK'
      <4>1. PICK m \\in sent :
             /\\ m.type = \"2a\"
             /\\ Send([type |-> \"2b\", bal |-> m.bal, val |-> m.val, acc |-> a])
        BY <3>4 DEF Phase2b
      <4>. QED BY <4>1, SMT DEF Inv, TypeOK, Send, Messages
    <3>. QED BY <2>1, <3>1, <3>2, <3>3, <3>4, Isa DEF Next
  <2>3. MsgInv'
    <3>1. ASSUME NEW b \\in Ballots, Phase1a(b) PROVE MsgInv'
      <4>1. \\A aa, vv, bb : VotedForIn(aa, vv, bb)' <=> VotedForIn(aa, vv, bb)
        BY <3>1 DEF Phase1a, Send, VotedForIn
      <4>. QED
        BY <2>2, <3>1, <4>1, SafeAtStable DEF Inv, MsgInv, TypeOK, Messages, Phase1a, Send
    <3>2. ASSUME NEW a \\in Acceptors, Phase1b(a) PROVE MsgInv'
      <4>0. PICK m \\in sent, r \\in last_voted(a) :
             /\\ m.type = \"1a\"
             /\\ \\A m2 \\in sent: m2.type \\in {\"1b\", \"2b\"} /\\ m2.acc = a => m.bal > m2.bal
             /\\ Send([type |-> \"1b\", bal |-> m.bal,
                      maxVBal |-> r.bal, maxVal |-> r.val, acc |-> a])
        BY <3>2 DEF Phase1b
      <4>1. \\A aa, vv, bb : VotedForIn(aa, vv, bb)' <=> VotedForIn(aa, vv, bb)
        BY <4>0 DEF Send, VotedForIn
      <4>. DEFINE mm == [type |-> \"1b\", bal |-> m.bal,
                         maxVBal |-> r.bal, maxVal |-> r.val, acc |-> a]
      <4>2. VotedForIn(mm.acc, mm.maxVal, mm.maxVBal) \\/ mm.maxVBal = -1
        BY <4>0, Isa DEF last_voted, VotedForIn
      <4>3. \\A c \\in (mm.maxVBal+1)..(mm.bal-1) :
               ~\\E v \\in Values : VotedForIn(mm.acc, v, c)
        BY <4>0, Isa DEF last_voted, VotedForIn
      <4>. QED
        BY <2>2, <3>2, <4>0, <4>1, <4>2, <4>3, SafeAtStable
           DEF Inv, MsgInv, TypeOK, Messages, Send
    <3>3. ASSUME NEW b \\in Ballots, Phase2a(b) PROVE MsgInv'
      <4>1. ~ \\E m \\in sent : (m.type = \"2a\") /\\ (m.bal = b)
        BY <3>3 DEF Phase2a
      <4>2. PICK v \\in Values, Q \\in Quorums,
                   S \\in SUBSET {m \\in sent : m.type = \"1b\" /\\ m.bal = b} :
               /\\ \\A a \\in Q : \\E m \\in S : m.acc = a
               /\\ \\/ \\A m \\in S : m.maxVBal = -1
                  \\/ \\E c \\in 0..(b-1) :
                       /\\ \\A m \\in S : m.maxVBal =< c
                       /\\ \\E m \\in S : /\\ m.maxVBal = c
                                       /\\ m.maxVal = v
               /\\ Send([type |-> \"2a\", bal |-> b, val |-> v])
        BY <3>3 DEF Phase2a
      <4>. DEFINE mm == [type |-> \"2a\", bal |-> b, val |-> v]
      <4>3. sent' = sent \\cup {mm}
        BY <4>2 DEF Send
      <4>4. \\A aa, vv, bb : VotedForIn(aa, vv, bb)' <=> VotedForIn(aa, vv, bb)
        BY <4>3 DEF VotedForIn
      <4>5. \\A ma \\in sent' : ma.type = \"2a\" /\\ ma.bal = mm.bal => ma = mm
        BY <4>1, <4>3 DEF Inv, MsgInv
      <4>6. SafeAt(v, b)
        <5>1. CASE \\A m \\in S : m.maxVBal = -1
          BY <4>2, <5>1, Isa DEF Inv, TypeOK, MsgInv, SafeAt, WontVoteIn, Messages
        <5>2. ASSUME NEW c \\in 0..(b-1),
                     \\A m \\in S : m.maxVBal =< c,
                     NEW ma \\in S, ma.maxVBal = c, ma.maxVal = v
              PROVE  SafeAt(v, b)
          <6> SUFFICES ASSUME NEW d \\in 0..(b-1)
                       PROVE  \\E QQ \\in Quorums : \\A q \\in QQ :
                                 VotedForIn(q, v, d) \\/ WontVoteIn(q, d)
            BY DEF SafeAt
          <6>1. CASE d \\in 0..(c-1)
            BY <5>2, <6>1, VotedInv, Isa DEF Inv, SafeAt, MsgInv, TypeOK, Messages
          <6>2. CASE d = c
            <7>1. VotedForIn(ma.acc, v, c)
              BY <4>2, <5>2, Isa DEF Inv, MsgInv
            <7>2. \\A q \\in Q, w \\in Values : VotedForIn(q, w, c) => w = v
              BY <7>1, <4>2, <5>2, VotedOnce, QuorumAssumption, Isa DEF Inv, TypeOK, Messages
            <7>3. \\A q \\in Q : WontVoteIn(q, c) \\/ VotedForIn(q, v, c)
              BY <4>2, <5>2, <6>2, <7>2, Isa DEF Inv, MsgInv, WontVoteIn, TypeOK, Messages
            <7>. QED BY <4>2, <7>3
          <6>3. CASE d \\in (c+1)..(b-1)
            BY <4>2, <5>2, <6>3, Isa DEF Inv, MsgInv, TypeOK, Messages, WontVoteIn
          <6>. QED BY <6>1, <6>2, <6>3
        <5>. QED BY <4>2, <5>1, <5>2
      <4>7. SafeAt(mm.val, mm.bal)'
        BY <2>2, <3>3, <4>6, SafeAtStable DEF Inv, Next
      <4>. QED
        BY <2>2, <3>3, <4>3, <4>4, <4>5, <4>7, SafeAtStable
           DEF Inv, MsgInv, TypeOK, Messages
    <3>4. ASSUME NEW a \\in Acceptors, Phase2b(a) PROVE MsgInv'
      <4>0. PICK m \\in sent :
             /\\ m.type = \"2a\"
             /\\ Send([type |-> \"2b\", bal |-> m.bal, val |-> m.val, acc |-> a])
        BY <3>4 DEF Phase2b
      <4>1. \\A aa, vv, bb : VotedForIn(aa, vv, bb)' <=>
                              VotedForIn(aa, vv, bb) \\/ (aa = a /\\ vv = m.val /\\ bb = m.bal)
        BY <4>0 DEF VotedForIn, Send
      <4>2. \\A mm \\in sent : mm.type = \"1b\"
               => \\A v \\in Values, c \\in (mm.maxVBal+1)..(mm.bal-1) :
                    ~ VotedForIn(mm.acc, v, c) => ~ VotedForIn(mm.acc, v, c)'
        BY <3>4, <4>0, <4>1, SMT DEF Phase2b, Inv, MsgInv, TypeOK, Messages
      <4>. QED
        BY <2>2, <3>4, <4>0, <4>1, <4>2, SafeAtStable, Isa DEF Inv, MsgInv, TypeOK, Messages, Send
    <3>. QED BY <2>1, <3>1, <3>2, <3>3, <3>4, Isa DEF Next
  <2>4. Inv'
    BY <2>2, <2>3 DEF Inv
  <2>5. CASE UNCHANGED vars
    BY <2>5, SMT DEF vars, Inv, TypeOK, MsgInv, VotedForIn, SafeAt, WontVoteIn
  <2>. QED BY <2>1, <2>4, <2>5, SMT DEF vars
<1>. QED BY <1>1, <1>2, PTL DEF Spec
'''
s=s[:start]+proof+s[end:]
p.write_text(s)
PY

[AGENT] I’ll make the interval/arithmetic consequences explicit, which should unblock the remaining quantified cases.

[CMD] /bin/zsh -lc "sed -n '240,390p' PaxosHistVar_Invariant.tla > /tmp/currentblock.txt
python3 - <<'PY'
from pathlib import Path
p=Path('PaxosHistVar_Invariant.tla')
s=p.read_text()
s=s.replace('BY SimpleArithmetic DEF mm','BY SMT DEF mm')
s=s.replace('<6>. QED BY <6>4, <6>5, SimpleArithmetic','<6>. QED BY <6>4, <6>5, SMT')
# replace maxVBal=-1 case with explicit proof
old='''        <5>1. CASE \\\\A m \\\\in S : m.maxVBal = -1
          BY <5>0, <5>1, AutoBlast DEF Inv, TypeOK, MsgInv, SafeAt, WontVoteIn, Messages
'''
new='''        <5>1. CASE \\\\A m \\\\in S : m.maxVBal = -1
          <6>1. \\\\E QQ \\\\in Quorums : \\\\A q \\\\in QQ : VotedForIn(q, v, d) \\\\/ WontVoteIn(q, d)
            <7>1. \\\\A q \\\\in Q : WontVoteIn(q, d)
              <8> SUFFICES ASSUME NEW q \\\\in Q PROVE WontVoteIn(q, d)
                BY Zenon
              <8>1. PICK mq \\\\in S : mq.acc = q
                BY <5>0
              <8>2. mq \\\\in sent /\\\\ mq.type = \"1b\" /\\\\ mq.bal = b /\\\\ mq.maxVBal = -1
                BY <4>2, <5>1, <8>1
              <8>3. d \\\\in (mq.maxVBal+1)..(mq.bal-1)
                BY <8>2, SMT
              <8>4. ~ \\\\E vv \\\\in Values : VotedForIn(q, vv, d)
                BY <8>2, <8>3 DEF Inv, MsgInv
              <8>5. \\\\E m0 \\\\in sent : m0.type \\\\in {\"1b\", \"2b\"} /\\\\ m0.acc = q /\\\\ m0.bal > d
                BY <8>2, SMT
              <8>. QED BY <8>4, <8>5 DEF WontVoteIn
            <7>. QED BY <5>0, <7>1
          <6>. QED BY <6>1
'''
s=s.replace(old,new)
# replace d=c case with more explicit? Try SMT/DEF including Inv for stubborn steps
s=s.replace('BY <5>0, <5>2, AutoBlast DEF Inv, MsgInv','BY <5>0, <5>2, SMT DEF Inv, MsgInv')
s=s.replace('BY <7>1, <5>0, <5>2, VotedOnce, QuorumAssumption, AutoBlast DEF Inv, TypeOK, Messages','BY <7>1, <5>0, <5>2, VotedOnce, QuorumAssumption, SMT DEF Inv, TypeOK, Messages')
s=s.replace('BY <5>0, <5>2, <6>2, <7>2, AutoBlast DEF Inv, MsgInv, WontVoteIn, TypeOK, Messages','BY <5>0, <5>2, <6>2, <7>2, SMT DEF Inv, MsgInv, WontVoteIn, TypeOK, Messages')
s=s.replace('BY <5>0, <5>2, <6>3, AutoBlast DEF Inv, MsgInv, TypeOK, Messages, WontVoteIn','BY <5>0, <5>2, <6>3, SMT DEF Inv, MsgInv, TypeOK, Messages, WontVoteIn')
s=s.replace('BY <5>0, <5>2, <6>1, VotedInv, AutoBlast DEF Inv, SafeAt, MsgInv, TypeOK, Messages','BY <5>0, <5>2, <6>1, VotedInv, SMT DEF Inv, SafeAt, MsgInv, TypeOK, Messages')
s=s.replace('BY <2>2, <3>4, <4>0, <4>1, <4>2, SafeAtStable, AutoBlast DEF Inv, MsgInv, TypeOK, Messages, Send','BY <2>2, <3>4, <4>0, <4>1, <4>2, SafeAtStable, SMT DEF Inv, MsgInv, TypeOK, Messages, Send')
s=s.replace('BY <2>1, <3>1, <3>2, <3>3, <3>4, AutoBlast DEF Next','BY <2>1, <3>1, <3>2, <3>3, <3>4, SMT DEF Next')

PY

[AGENT] I’ll make the final `Next` dispatch explicit and switch the arithmetic contradiction to Isabelle.

[CMD] /bin/zsh -lc "python3 - <<'PY'
from pathlib import Path
p=Path('PaxosHistVar_Invariant.tla')
s=p.read_text()
s=s.replace('''          <6>5. mm.maxVBal = r.bal
            BY DEF mm
          <6>6. c > r.bal
            BY <6>5, SimpleArithmetic
          <6>. QED BY <6>4, <6>6, SimpleArithmetic''','''          <6>5. c \\\\in (r.bal+1)..(m.bal-1)
            BY DEF mm
          <6>6. c > r.bal
            BY <6>5, Isa
          <6>. QED BY <6>4, <6>6, Isa''')
s=s.replace('''    <3>. QED BY <2>1, <3>1, <3>2, <3>3, <3>4, SMT DEF Next
  <2>3. MsgInv' ''','''    <3>5. ASSUME \\\\E b \\\\in Ballots : Phase1a(b) \\\\/ Phase2a(b)
          PROVE TypeOK'
      <4>1. PICK b \\\\in Ballots : Phase1a(b) \\\\/ Phase2a(b)
        BY <3>5
      <4>2. CASE Phase1a(b)
        BY <3>1, <4>2
      <4>3. CASE Phase2a(b)
        BY <3>2, <4>3
      <4>. QED BY <4>1, <4>2, <4>3
    <3>6. ASSUME \\\\E a \\\\in Acceptors : Phase1b(a) \\\\/ Phase2b(a)
          PROVE TypeOK'
      <4>1. PICK a \\\\in Acceptors : Phase1b(a) \\\\/ Phase2b(a)
        BY <3>6
      <4>2. CASE Phase1b(a)
        BY <3>3, <4>2
      <4>3. CASE Phase2b(a)
        BY <3>4, <4>3
      <4>. QED BY <4>1, <4>2, <4>3
    <3>. QED BY <2>1, <3>5, <3>6 DEF Next
  <2>3. MsgInv' ''')
p.write_text(s)
PY

[CMD] /bin/zsh -lc "cat > /tmp/DisjTest.tla <<'EOF'
---- MODULE DisjTest ----
EXTENDS TLAPS
CONSTANTS S, T
A == \\E x \\in S : TRUE
B == \\E y \\in T : TRUE
N == \\/ A
     \\/ B
THEOREM T1 == ASSUME N,
                     A => TRUE,
                     B => TRUE
              PROVE TRUE
BY DEF N
THEOREM T2 == ASSUME N
              PROVE A \\/ B
BY DEF N
====
EOF
